Each package is independently versioned with a protobuf semantic\n12: versioning scheme based on https://cloud.google.com/apis/design/versioning.\n13: \n14: The major version for a package is captured in its name (and directory structure). Multiple resource\n27:   type URLs may be managed by a single muxer. protocols. Key findings:\\n\\n**Type URL to Service Mapping (source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc):** This file implements the critical conversion from resource type URLs (e.g., 'type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.route.v3.RouteConfiguration') to v3 gRPC service methods. The typeUrlToV3ServiceMap() function explicitly enumerates all v3 service discovery services including RouteDiscoveryService, ClusterDiscoveryService, EndpointDiscoveryService, ListenerDiscoveryService, RuntimeDiscoveryService, SecretDiscoveryService, ScopedRoutesDiscoveryService, VirtualHostDiscoveryService, LocalityEndpointDiscoveryService, and ExtensionConfigDiscoveryService. Functions deltaGrpcMethod() and sotwGrpcMethod() map resource types to their respective gRPC endpoints.\\n\\n**ADS gRPC Server and Mux Implementation:** The xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc implements both GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta classes that inherit from GrpcMuxImpl. The dual-version subscription handling multiplexes multiple resource subscriptions on a single gRPC stream.\\n\\n**Subscription State Management:** The sotw_subscription_state.cc implements SotwSubscriptionState which inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse, envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest>. The handleGoodResponse() function processes v3 DiscoveryResponse messages. Similarly, delta_subscription_state.h/.cc in the xds_mux directory implements DeltaSubscriptionState for delta protocol handling with v3 DeltaDiscoveryResponse/DeltaDiscoveryRequest types. The addResourceStateFromServer() function processes v3 Resource messages from delta responses.\\n\\n**v2 to v3 Versioning:** The utility.h file contains checkTransportVersion() which validates and enforces v3-only transport (V2 is deprecated). The api_version.h defines ApiVersion enum with V2 (deprecated, value 1) and V3 (value 2).
